Our country's telecom industry has been subjected to the incompetence of bureaucratic politics on one hand and the influence of a bad system on the other for more than fifty years, resulting in a fragmented situation, and now it has reached the brink of survival. Unexpectedly, the postal service, which has been beyond the turbulence of political tides for more than thirty years, has not been ruined during the days when foreign ministers were in power, but has been shaken after the recovery of postal rights. Our association and others are deeply saddened by the imminent collapse of the telecom administration and are striving to struggle. We cannot bear to see the postal service become a sequel to the telecom administration. Now, the Ministry of Transportation has not adopted the suggestions of the postal workers, which has led to the realization of the most unfortunate postal strike. Postal and telecom workers stand on the same ground and should do their best to provide active assistance. We also hope that all compatriots across the country will recognize that the rise and fall of transportation enterprises are related to the national economy and the people's livelihood, and will unanimously support and urge the authorities to adopt the suggestions quickly, so as to prevent the storm from expanding and becoming more difficult to control. Transportation is fortunate, and the country is fortunate. This declaration is hereby made. The Telecom Workers' Unions of Fujian, Hebei, Jiangsu, etc."

THE JAPANESE TRANSPORT SHIP GUANGFU MARU CAUGHT FIRE YESTERDAY 47

All the gasoline inside the ship was destroyed

The fire spread rapidly

The Japanese army and navy have been withdrawing successively in recent days. The Japanese Ministry of the Army specially dispatched several military transport ships to Shanghai to transport troops. The ships "Yemaru" and "Guanganmaru," among others, were used. Yesterday, the Japanese 9th Division's Akazawa Brigade, the Military Police Corps, and a large amount of ammunition were withdrawn from Shanghai and transported by the transport ship "Haianmaru," escorted by a torpedo boat of the 26th Japanese Naval Unit. There was also a Japanese transport ship named "Guangfumaru," carrying a large amount of airplane gasoline and other items, anchored on the Jiangmian River surface near the Lantian Factory pier in the eastern section of Yangshupu. Yesterday afternoon, the ship suddenly caught fire. Because the cabin was full of gasoline, which is highly flammable, the fire spread rapidly once ignited. In an instant, the fire became fierce and unapproachable. Although the personnel on board tried their best to extinguish the fire with specially prepared fire extinguishing chemicals, they were ineffective due to the excessive flames. The ship owners and others sent a telegram seeking help. The Japanese navy warships rushed to help after hearing the news. The Fire Brigade was notified and immediately dispatched a small boat carrying a fire engine to put out the fire. Until 6:00 p.m., the fire was not completely extinguished, but it had been slightly suppressed. Most of the military gasoline and other items carried on the ship were lost, and the ship's hull was also damaged. The Japanese military authorities are investigating.

SHIRAKAWA'S CONDITION REMAINS CRITICAL 48

Unable to eat, breathing rapidly

No change in Shigemitsu Aoi yesterday

The condition of Japanese Commander Shirakawa remained critical yesterday. His breathing became more rapid, and he was unable to eat anything. The Japanese Army Hospital believes that his condition is not optimistic. Yesterday morning, Shirakawa's condition was reported as: body temperature 37.6, pulse 90, respiration 17. In the afternoon, his condition was: body temperature 37, pulse 82, respiration 14. The Zhenfu Min Hospital reported yesterday that there was no change in Minister Shigemitsu's injuries.

STRANGE COLORED WHITE CLOUDS IN THE SKY YESTERDAY EVENING 49

Shaped like dancing ribbons, colored silver-gray

Chinese and foreign men and women looked up in amazement

The weather was clear yesterday. At 6:45 p.m., a white cloud suddenly appeared in the sky, winding like a stage ribbon, shining brightly in a silver-gray color. At the time, the sun had already set, but the light had not yet disappeared. The sky was a sheet of blue, with no clouds at all. Chinese and foreign men and women in the streets stopped and looked up in amazement, calling it a white dragon. Yesterday evening, when the sun set, strange colored white clouds suddenly appeared in the sky. Villagers in Baoshan Yuepu and other places mistakenly thought it was a lunar eclipse and followed the old custom of setting off firecrackers. For a time, the sound of firecrackers was loud. The Japanese army stationed in Yanghang was greatly alarmed when they heard the sound and immediately dug trenches, tightened security, and deployed defenses. The situation was very serious. Later, they realized it was a misunderstanding and restored the original state.

THE SEVERITY OF THE DROUGHT DISASTER 52

Zhang also telegraphed that since last year, there has been very little rain in Shaanxi and Gansu. After entering winter, black frost suddenly fell. The drought is even more severe this year. The cotton and wheat planted by the farmers have all withered and died. There is a shortage of food, and disaster victims are everywhere. The problem of people's food has already caused a great panic. Now, every hundred catties of flour has risen to more than fifteen yuan, and every dou of wheat has risen to three yuan and five jiao, and there is a continued rapid increase. The disaster area is gradually expanding, and the number of disaster victims is increasing day by day. The people are clamoring for food. The disaster area is gradually expanding, and all the wheat is dried and dead. Autumn seedlings cannot be sown, and the land has also lost its effectiveness. Director Yang Hucheng has telegraphed the capital to ask for relief and, on the one hand, to appease the people and discuss relief methods. It will not be effective without widely asking for relief.

APPEAL TO CHARITABLE ORGANIZATIONS 53

He earnestly requested Mr. Li Rongbin and Mr. Hu Shuhua to discuss and launch emergency relief. However, no matter what charitable organization it is, it is best to go directly to provide relief. Relief funds and relief goods do not have to go through any agency, so that relief can be provided one day earlier, and more disaster victims can live. If it is possible to use the development of the Northwest industry and work relief, thereby using the dying cheap labor force to build projects, build roads, and exploit minerals, etc., then disaster relief and the revitalization of industry will be accomplished, and one move will have multiple benefits.

JAPANESE SENTRY SHOOTS AND WOUNDS A BOATMAN AND HIS WIFE 57

Zhang Changyu's life is in danger

There is a fishing boat moored in the Yangjingzhen River opposite the Dagong Yarn Factory in Yangshupu. The boatman is an old couple from Jiangbei, named Zhang Changyu, 50 years old, and his wife, Zhou, 42 years old, who depend on each other for life. Last night at 11:30, they were awakened from their sleep by the noise in the area and went ashore together to investigate. Unexpectedly, there was a Japanese army camp stationed across the shore, and they were seen by the Japanese army sentries, who opened fire many times. One bullet hit Zhang in the throat, and the bullet pierced through. His breath was barely continuing. Another bullet hit Zhou's left breast. Later, neighbors who heard the news arrived and sent them to Renji Hospital for treatment. According to the doctor, Zhang's life is in danger due to his age and weak blood. The hospital then notified the Fourth Horse Road Police Station, which ordered two Western detectives to go to the hospital to investigate and report to the police chief for handling.

The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Society has determined that the Jiading area has been ravaged by the Japanese army this time, and the disaster situation is extremely serious. Each member will conduct on-site investigations with the local district chiefs and village chiefs, select the most impoverished, and give them foreign rice separately. Also, the houses of the villagers in various places have been either bombed or burned, leaving them homeless, which is especially tragic. Therefore, in the northeast and two townships of Jiading and the Loutang area, those who are the most helpless will be lent funds to build thatched houses, so that they can temporarily have a place to live. A total of 4,000 yuan has been issued. The above two matters are now nearing completion. However, after inspecting the disaster area, the disaster situation is extremely serious, and the association has a sense of using a cup of water to put out a fire. It is hoped that charitable magnates will donate generously so that the work can be carried out and the disaster victims can be helped.

THE MUNICIPAL POLICE BUREAU CRACKS DOWN ON A LARGE BATCH OF MILITARY WEAPONS 61

Various firearms and bullets were seized

More than a dozen criminals have been arrested

Lu Ying, the captain of the Detective Team of the Municipal Police Bureau, received a secret report from detectives Wu Kezhong, Zhao Huairen, and Chen Caifu that arms dealers Zhang Zaixiang, Liu Zihan, and others were hiding in the Nanshi area and had set up more than four organizations. After receiving the report, Captain Lu dispatched detectives Dan Bin, Cui Youkuan, and Liu Xiangyun, along with secret agents Yang Qing and You Hanwen, at 8:00 p.m. on the 21st, to join forces with the police officers of the Second District to the 59th lane of Zhenxinmingli in the Shanghai Army Camp, No. 5 Yangchang Lane outside Dananmen, No. 2, 29 Lane, Fushan Tang Street and No. 150, Lixian Gua Street and other places. More than ten male and female criminals, including Zhang Zaixiang, were arrested, and twelve rifles, one submachine gun, three large boxes of bullets, four bullet belts, four empty wooden shells, and about 3,650 scattered bullets, as well as many parts for the guns, were seized and taken away for strict interrogation and investigation. After hearing the news, Zhang Dongkai, the district chief of the Second District of the Bureau, dispatched Liu Xueli, the patrol chief of the Chenjiaqiao Police Station, and police officer Sun Changrong to Xinmingli, Miaojiang Road, at 11:00 p.m. on the same day. Li Guangqin, the account room manager, led them to an empty house at No. 27, where six large and small wooden boxes were found. Inside, there was one Jinling-made small submachine gun, one Shanghai-made submachine gun body, five bolt-action rifles, five Hanyang-made rifles, two Guangdong-made rifles, one Type 38 rifle, seven bolt-action iron sleeves, twelve bullet slots, twenty-six submachine gun barrels, two rifles, three boxes of rifle bullets, about 5,000 rounds, and a package of rifle parts. District Chief Zhang believed that the matter concerned the private storage of military weapons and immediately submitted the evidence to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for review.

HONGXING COMPANY SUES DOU YANONG FOR NON-PAYMENT OF RENT 62

Mediation breaks down, rehearing scheduled

Dou Yanong from Shandong is a current military officer who participated in the Sino-Japanese Songhu Battle. His family lives in the middle section of Ningbo Road. Recently, due to the fact that all citizens were affected by the war, a movement to reduce and exempt rent was launched. A Rent Reduction and Exemption Movement Committee was organized, and it was resolved that all places north of the Suzhou River should be exempt from rent for three months, and all places south of the Suzhou River should be exempt for two months. The house where Dou lived was the property of the Hongxing Company. The rent from November of last year to April of this year has not been paid. The owner asked him to pay, and Dou told him that the rent for November and December was old debt and should be paid. The rent for January and April should also be repaid in installments. However, the Rent Reduction Committee has already resolved to exempt the rent for February and March, and has submitted it to the Social Affairs Bureau for review. Before the approval is received, it would be different from everyone else to pay first, and to destroy unity. The rent for these two months is difficult to pay at this time. The owner then extended the lawsuit to the First Special District Local Court through lawyers Yan and Sen. Judge Lou held a court session and persuaded both parties to resolve the matter peacefully out of court. However, although the host and guests contacted each other repeatedly, they did not reach an agreement. Yesterday, Judge Lou continued the hearing and advised both parties to resolve the matter peacefully in court. He ordered the defendant to pay the rent for November and December, and the rent for January and April to be returned in four months, namely June, July, October and November. Dou also obeyed. As for the remaining two months of February and March, Dou intended to wait for the Social Affairs Bureau to resolve the rent reduction issue and then settle the account. The plaintiff argued that it should also be repaid in installments. If the Social Affairs Bureau approves the rent exemption for the two months in the future, the plaintiff can return it. However, Dou strongly opposed this argument. Although Judge Lou earnestly advised, neither party showed any concession, and the mediation broke down again. Therefore, it was ordered to reschedule the hearing for further review.

Feng Sulan accuses Cao Zhimei of seduction and abandonment 63

Demanding 20,000 yuan for damages and living expenses

Feng Sulan, a local woman also known as Meidi, is twenty years old, quite attractive, and lives at No. 128 Feihong Road. She formerly studied at Yangzheng Girls' School in the city and was of excellent character and academics. Recently, she engaged lawyer Tang Huaiqun to file a complaint with the First Special District Court against Cao Zhimei, residing at No. 47 Tongzhou Road, for seduction, intimidation, and abandonment. The afternoon before yesterday, Judge Wu Tingqi presided over a joint hearing in the Second Criminal Court. The defendant, Cao Zhimei, failed to appear despite being summoned. According to the plaintiff's representative, lawyer Tang Huaiqun, since the defendant failed to appear, he requested an arrest warrant. Subsequently, the plaintiff, Feng Sulan, presented herself. Feng was wearing a white-based, light red floral cheongsam, silk stockings, and leather shoes. Standing in the witness stand, she calmly recounted her love affair, appearing relaxed and not at all embarrassed. She claimed that since she was young, her parents had arranged a marriage for her with someone else, and the wedding was originally scheduled for the eighth day of the fifth lunar month of the year before last. However, in the first month of the same year, she happened to visit Little World in the city and met the defendant, who used all sorts of enticements and sweet words. At that time, she was eighteen years old and easily influenced, so she was seduced and taken to a hotel, where they engaged in sexual relations. The defendant claimed to be unmarried and willing to commit to a lifelong relationship, which she believed to be true. Later, as her wedding date approached, the defendant came to see her again, threatening suicide and demanding that she leave her family. He repeatedly incited her to take all the engagement gifts, including jewelry, and hide at No. 325 Changan Lane, Xinji Bang Road, to live together. Afterwards, she heard that her parents and the groom's family had agreed to dissolve the engagement, so she felt even more uninhibited in her relationship with the defendant. In January of last year, the defendant was involved in a property dispute with his sister and lacked funds to cover all the expenses. He tactfully asked her for help, claiming that she was also involved in the matter. She sold all her jewelry to help him with the lawsuit. Unexpectedly, about ten days later, a woman came to her, hurling insults and claiming to be the defendant's wife. Others persuaded her to leave. From then on, she realized that she had been completely fooled by the defendant. She could only endure and reflect on her situation. She seized an opportunity to question the defendant, who claimed that the woman wanted a divorce and that he truly wished to marry her. He promised that once the lawsuit was over, he would hand over the property deed to her. He said that the woman was merely a wife in name only. Since things had already progressed too far, she felt there was nothing she could do. Later, the defendant planned to open a confectionery shop in Hongzhen and, lacking capital, pleaded with her for help. Considering that they couldn't simply live off her savings, she sold all her remaining jewelry and gave him 900 yuan in installments. In December of the same year, the defendant claimed that he had won the lawsuit and had been awarded a house (the current address at No. 47 Tongzhou Road). After several months, the defendant's behavior changed drastically. Because she thought that their love was not yet broken, she could only be patient. However, the defendant showed no consideration. At first, he would not visit for ten days, then he would disappear for half a month. Since the war in Shanghai started, she was living in the war zone. All the neighbors moved away, leaving her alone in the midst of gunfire, while the defendant never came to comfort her, treating her as if she were a stranger. When they occasionally met, he would insult her with harsh words, completely reversing his previous attitude, and making all kinds of threats, saying that he wanted to kill her. This behavior showed a complete break in their relationship, making it impossible to continue their relationship. Therefore, she filed a lawsuit, demanding that he be punished according to the law and, in addition, filed a civil suit, demanding the return of the 3,000 yuan in clothing, jewelry, and personal savings that she had been deceived out of, as well as all the damages and future living expenses, totaling 20,000 yuan. Judge Wu examined the testimony and, since the defendant was not present, he adjourned the case and ordered the defendant to be summoned for questioning at a later date.

Chen Weiru acquitted 64

Chen Weiru, a compradore from Yangzhou working for the Jia Li Foreign Firm on Jiangxi Road, was previously accused of defrauding the China Industrial Bank of 14,000 taels of silver under the guise of being a compradore for the foreign firm. The defendant hired lawyer Tang Mingshi to represent him. After the interrogation was completed, Chief Judge Qian Hongye of the First Criminal Court declared the defendant Chen Weiru not guilty the morning before yesterday. The private prosecution brought by the China Industrial Bank was rejected, and the related civil lawsuit was transferred to the Civil Court of this court for adjudication.

Gun Tax Company discovered in the French Concession 65

Scheduled to begin on the 25th of this month

Since French Consul General Meyrier and Chief Inspector Février took over the French Concession, they have placed the greatest importance on suppressing opium smoking. For several months, they have cracked down on at least a dozen opium cases every day, and recently, they seem to have completely eradicated the practice. Yesterday at 3:00 PM, a reporter from this newspaper was passing by the entrance of Bulin Lane on Zhengjia Muqiao, Avenue Edward VII, when he noticed many strangely dressed men standing there, all looking happy and discussing something animatedly. Upon entering the lane, he saw a black leather sign about two feet long with gold letters on the wall of No. 8 in the lane, which read "Security Company." A young man pointed to the reporter and said, "This is the newly created cigarette pipe tax company resurrected." It was established today (the 22nd). Entering the building, he saw ten wooden counters lined up facing each other, each with a writing desk inside. Two young men were sitting opposite each other. In the corner of the east wall, there was a blackboard with a notice posted on it, which read, "To whom it may concern, all the regulations of this company have already been announced and registration has begun. Anyone who wants to know the details can inquire at the information desk." Below the notice was an oval stamp with the words "Security Company Bingji Stamp 5/23." When asked about the company's founders by two people who appeared to be employees, they said that the company had just been established today and that registration would begin tomorrow (the 23rd). The registration fee is 3.5 yuan for one to five guns and 7 yuan for one to ten guns. Then, starting from the 25th of this month, a fee of five yuan in silver dollars will be charged per gun per day. When asked who founded the company, they were vague. In the evening, when inquiring at the police station, it was learned that there was no such illegal company. It is said that after learning of this, the police station has reported it to the Commissioner of Police and is strictly banning it.

Central Bank Inspection Report 66

125th Time

The 125th inspection report of the issuance reserve of the Central Bank states: According to Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve of the exchange notes issued by this bank. On May 20th of the 21st year of the Republic of China, Inspector Yu Zhiqing conducted the 125th inspection at the Issuance Bureau of this bank. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) Total amount of exchange notes issued: 27,665,604 silver dollars, including 24,925,192 silver dollar notes and 2,740,412 subsidiary currency notes. Total amount of exchange note reserve: 27,665,604 silver dollars, including 22,126,328 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 19,043,979.45 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing treasury, 1,433,257 silver dollars stored in branches in various ports, and 1,649,091.55 silver dollars stored in peer banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 5,539,276 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold exchange notes issued: 375,000 customs gold units. Total amount of customs gold exchange note reserve: 375,000 customs gold units. This reserve includes 150,000 US dollars, stored in a peer bank in this city, at a fixed exchange rate of 40 units to the customs gold unit. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Exchange Note Regulations, 60% of the reserve should be in cash and 40% should be in guarantee. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. Central Bank Board of Supervisors, May 20th, 21st year of the Republic of China.

The Executive Yuan responds to the impeachment of Wang Jingwei 72

Stating that the signing of the agreement was resolved by the Political Council

Therefore, there is no need to submit it to the Legislative Yuan

(Nanjing) Regarding the fact that the Control Yuan has impeached Executive Yuan President Wang for signing the truce agreement without the approval of the Legislative Yuan, a reporter from this newspaper visited Executive Yuan Secretary-General Chu Minyi to inquire about the details. According to Chu, on May 3rd, the Central Political Council, President Wang reported on the Shanghai Truce and Withdrawal Agreement. The Central Political Council resolved to pass it. President Wang continued to ask whether the case should be submitted to the Legislative Yuan. The Central Political Council resolved that it did not need to be submitted to the Legislative Yuan. The Central Political Council is the highest political organ of our party. Since there is the above resolution, the agreement does not need to be submitted to the Legislative Yuan. (Special dispatch, 22nd)

(Nanjing) After the Control Yuan's memorial to impeach Wang Jingwei was issued yesterday, it stated that political leaders in various rule-of-law countries are always subject to questioning and impeachment. Those involved should have ample opportunity to respond and should be allowed to publish their responses. The telegram bureau should not withhold their messages, so as to conform to the spirit of the rule of law. Therefore, telegrams to other cities were sent after midnight. The newspapers in this city did not have time to print them. The Executive Yuan stated that since war had not been declared, there could be no negotiation. The Shanghai Truce and Withdrawal Agreement had been reported to the Central Political Council by the Executive Yuan and passed without objection. Moreover, it had been repeatedly stated in advance that the agreement did not have any political conditions attached and was entirely an administrative procedure. Therefore, there was no need to submit it to the Legislative Yuan for resolution. If there were political conditions attached, it would have been submitted to the Legislative Yuan for resolution long ago. (Special dispatch, 22nd)

(Nanjing) The original case of the Control Yuan's impeachment of Wang Jingwei was proposed by member Gao Youtang, who stated that the signing of the truce agreement without submitting it to the Legislative Yuan for resolution was an inexcusable violation of the law. The Executive Yuan's autocratic and arbitrary actions are of minor importance, but opening this bad precedent would be very dangerous in the future. If not severely punished, then in the future, with regard to national sovereignty and territory, there would be a precedent to follow, and all would be given away under the words "agreement." In order to prevent problems before they arise, he proposed impeachment. After the court handed it over to members Liu San and others for review, they reported that the members believed that since the country is called a rule of law, all measures should follow the rule of law. On the contrary, it is a violation of the law and should be subject to the sanctions of the law. The Organic Law of the National Government stipulates that the Legislative Yuan has the power to resolve declarations of war, peace, and other important international matters. Although this truce agreement is different from a declaration of war or peace, it is undoubtedly an international matter. The Executive Yuan signed it without submitting it to the Legislative Yuan for resolution, which is a clear violation of the law. Moreover, things are always changing. In the future, external precedents can be agreed upon at will, and the dangers cannot be overstated. Member Gao's application for punishment is indeed appropriate. After receiving the report, the court presented it to the Central Supervisory Committee members to propose impeachment in accordance with Article 10, Section 1 of Chapter 3 of the Civil Servant Disciplinary Act, and the entire case was announced on the afternoon of the 21st. (Special dispatch, 22nd)

Tang Ke san talks about the negotiation process 81

(Nanjing) Tang Ke San returned to Beijing yesterday and talked about the occurrence of the Kang Tibetan dispute. The Dalai Lama telegraphed the central government, asking to send personnel familiar with the Tibetan situation to Kang to handle the matter, and stated that he had ordered the Da Jin side to stop military action and return to their original defense. I started on April 3rd of last year. When I arrived in Chongqing, I suddenly heard that the Tibetan army had occupied Ganzi. When I arrived in Chengdu, I heard that the Tibetan army had occupied Zhanhua. I couldn't succeed with my bare hands. I telegraphed asking the Dalai Lama to withdraw his troops. In June, I arrived in Kangding and learned that the Dalai Lama had sent Changdu Kalon as his representative and Qiong Rang Daiben to Ganzi to negotiate. On July 8th, I arrived in Lhuo and sent Liu Yuan to Gan to connect with Qiong Rang to retreat the Gan Zhan Tibetan army, and to urge the Kalon to come to Gan to meet. Unexpectedly, Qiong and others delayed for reasons and never fulfilled the promise of retreat, negotiating for more than a month and only agreeing to go to Dege, while the troops in Gan Zhan still did not withdraw. I secretly reported to the central government and requested that the three provinces of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Qing be ordered to use force to recover, not only to recover Gan Zhan, but also to restore the entire Kang. Before the joint efforts, it was proposed that Liu Chengxun send a brigade of troops and use the Zhan Ding militia. I went to Gan first to negotiate with the Tibetan side, but Liu was unable to implement it for some reason. At that time, the central government was dealing with Shi Yousan's rebellion and had no time to take care of the southwestern incident, so it could not be implemented. I could not exercise my power in Lhuo, nor could I command the troops. Empty negotiations were of no avail. After dragging on for several months, when the Northeast Incident occurred, the Dalai Lama took the opportunity to urgently request the central government to discuss the Dabai incident first, and other issues would be handled separately. I argued that border defense relations were important and argued that it was impossible. Because Dabai is all under the jurisdiction of Ganzi, and Gan Zhan is the gateway to Xikang. If we don't try to recover it, the gateway will be lost and Kang will be in danger. I repeatedly telegraphed, rather than only discussing Dabai and not talking about Gan Zhan, it would be better to leave them all as pending cases, and order the Sichuan army to firmly defend the current defense, and wait for the Sino Japanese incident to settle down before handling it. As a result, the Tibetan side spread rumors, saying that it had already been handled with the central government, causing the people of the four counties of Gan Jian Zhan Li to panic and express their unwillingness to return to Tibet. If only Dabai is discussed and Ganzi is discussed in depth, then the entire Kang will be shaken from the roots. I requested to resign from the central government due to the difficulty in handling the matter, and another virtuous person was sent. I was not approved. In order to seek perfection, I negotiated with the Tibetan representative Qiong Rang, and in accordance with the central government's intentions, I formulated ten conditions for peace with Tibet, which were approved by the central government, but the Tibetan side expressed opposition in the middle of the way, resulting in a breakdown. At that time, I had become the target of public criticism, and the Kang people also referred to me as an envoy to cede land. My old illness recurred, and I asked to resign again. Fortunately, I was approved and General Liu Jun was sent to handle it with full authority. On the 20th of last month, the handover was completed and I set off to return to Beijing. When I arrived in Chengdu, I learned that Gesang Zeren had invaded Batang and shot and killed Brigade Commander Ma, and Kangnan was also in an emergency. Now Liu has sent Brigade Commander Yu to defend it. Recently, I received a telegram from General Liu Jun, stating that Gan Zhan had been captured. Of the thirty-three counties in Xikang, six or seven have been divided. If there is no way to solve it, not only will the proposal to establish a province be disappointed, but in a year, there will be no land left in Xikang. (Special dispatch, 22nd)

Draft of Kang Tibetan Peace Conditions 82

(Nanjing) The ten drafts of Kang Tibetan Peace Conditions are as follows: Article 1. Now we follow the central government's telegram order to seek Kang Tibetan peace. Ganzi and Zhanhua are temporarily stationed by Tibetan troops, and will be handled separately in the future. According to this article, it is based on the central government's and the Dalai Lama's direct agreement and telegram order, and there is no room for consultation in Gan, so it is stipulated as above. Article 2. After the Dabai case is completed by impartial handling this time, the Qiong Rang representative will be responsible for ensuring that this kind of thing does not happen again. According to the peace conditions, the contract must be signed after the Dabai case is concluded. The case is judged by Qiong Rang, and our side monitors it. If it is unfair, our side can refuse to sign the contract, and there are six other measures to settle Dabai, which are attached later.

Article 3. The Kang party will station 200 troops in Lhuo and Daofu, and the Tibetan party will station 200 troops in Ganzi and Zhanhua. The rest will be withdrawn, and the two parties shall not initiate conflicts without authorization. If any party causes trouble, the government will handle it. The reason for the incident will be announced and testified by the central committee member in the government meeting.

Article 4. Qiongxia two villages still belong to Lihua, and Zhu Wo originally belonged to Lhuo, and will be returned.

Article 5. More than 77,000 taels of silver owed by the Dajin Temple to the Lhucheng Chamber of Commerce will be ordered by Qiong Rang Daiben to be returned quickly by the temple. According to this article, a method of repaying the money in installments has been proposed. At the end of the lunar year, 20,000 taels will be repaid first, 20,000 taels will be repaid at the end of February next year, 20,000 taels will be repaid at the end of April, and the payment will be cleared at the end of June.

Article 6. Jia Ben Abo Bu and other two people from Bai Qu will return to Gan and wait for Qiong Rang to judge impartially. The Tibetan party shall not abuse them in the slightest. If there are things that hinder freedom and damage their lives, after the judgment is completed, Qiong Rang will report to the Dalai Lama, and the central committee member will also report to the government and the conference in the same way. After this case is concluded, the Tibetan party shall treat the people of Bai Li equally.

Article 7. The Tibetan party once gave the captured Sichuan army food and clothing. The central committee member will discuss with the Sichuan government to allocate money to return it and release them all. According to this article, the Tibetan party gave more than 130 captured soldiers food and clothing for one year, and Zhang Zhishi and others have lived there for several years, and have paid for it. They requested that it be returned. Zhang Zhishi has now been sent back first. The captured soldiers will not be released until the money is returned. After further consultations, it was agreed that 20,000 Tibetan oceans, totaling more than 8,000 silver dollars, would be included in the text of the agreement when it is formally signed.

Article 8. Brigade Commander Ma and Qiong Niang Daiben will send people to meet each other to explain the previous suspicion.

Article 9. Restore transportation and protect commerce. The Chinese and merchants stationed in Tibet who go to Lhucheng for trade will be treated equally by both parties.

Article 10. The above nine articles are temporary truce conditions. All Kang Tibetan issues will be handled separately. If there is any ambiguity in the interpretation of the articles, Chinese shall prevail.

It has been found that there were a total of eight original conditions, and then Article 6 and Article 10 were added, making a total of ten. They have been sent separately to the Mongolian Tibetan Committee General Liu Jun for review, and this will be the standard when it is formally signed. This is hereby declared. (Special dispatch, 22nd)

Foreign Telegrams

Viscount Saitō Entrusted with Forming a Cabinet 118

The End of Party Rule in Japan

A Transcendent Cabinet Finally Realized

Selection of Cabinet Members Still Requires Some Time

Ishii Tentatively Appointed as Foreign Minister, Wakatsuki as Finance Minister

United Press Agency, Tokyo, 22nd: Prince Saionji entered the palace to see the Emperor at 1:27 PM today, recommending Viscount Saitō Makoto as the next Prime Minister. Saitō was summoned to the palace at 6:35 PM to receive the order to form a cabinet. After leaving the palace, he immediately telegraphed Count Kodama Hideo, the former Director-General of Korean Affairs, and Tsurukichi Maruyama, the former Superintendent-General of the Metropolitan Police, to discuss the principles for organizing a new cabinet. He scheduled to meet with Suzuki, the President of the Seiyukai, and Wakatsuki, the President of the Minseitō, tomorrow morning to discuss cabinet formation and requested that both presidents join the cabinet to jointly save the current crisis.

Reuters, Tokyo, 22nd: Count Kodama told reporters after meeting with the new Prime Minister Saitō today that the Prime Minister intends to consult with Elder Prince Saionji on the formation of the new cabinet tomorrow and seek his understanding. It is expected that the composition of the new cabinet will take as long as a week, as the situation is extremely complicated and requires extremely careful consideration. It is widely believed that Saitō may invite Viscount Ishii to serve as Foreign Minister and Wakatsuki to serve as Finance Minister. The Navy Ministry has already tentatively nominated Admiral Okada to serve as Navy Minister.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 22nd: Who will be the Minister of the Army in the Saitō Cabinet is most noteworthy. Army Minister Araki may remain in office due to the sincere wishes of Chief of Staff Masaki, Commander of the Military Police Qin, and other military officials. As for the post of Navy Minister, Admiral Abo is the most likely candidate.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 22nd: Saitō has begun forming his cabinet at his private residence in Yotsuya Nakamachi, designating former Superintendent-General of the Metropolitan Police Tsurukichi Maruyama as Cabinet Secretary. Count Kodama Hideo also appears likely to join the cabinet.

Saitō's Brief Biography 119

Viscount Saitō was born in Iwate Prefecture in 1858 and is currently 74 years old. He was poor in his youth (and served as a clerk in the Navy Department, the same as Hara Takashi and Gotō Shinpei, and later all three rose to high positions, which is considered a beautiful story). Through diligence and learning, he gradually rose to his current position and is even hailed as one of the three great men of Tohoku in modern Japan, along with Hara Takashi and Gotō Shinpei. He was appointed a Navy Ensign in 1882 and promoted to Navy Admiral in 1906. During this time, he served as a military aide, captain of the Akitsushima and Izumo ships. When Yamamoto was Navy Minister, Saitō served as Vice Minister. From 1906, he successively served as Navy Minister in the Saionji, Katsura, and Yamamoto cabinets for a total of eight years. In 1913, he resigned due to the naval bribery scandal and was incorporated into the reserve army. In 1919, the Hara cabinet was formed, and he accepted Hara Takashi's trust and served as Governor-General of Korea. After the March 1st Movement (the Korean independence movement in the Republic of China in 1919), he strongly advocated abolishing the policy of military rule. He was granted the title of Viscount in 1907. In 1927, he served as the chief representative of the Geneva Naval Disarmament Conference. After returning home, he resigned as Governor-General of Korea and became a Privy Councilor. In 1929, he accepted

Saitō, Who Was Ordered to Form a Cabinet 120

Prime Minister Hamaguchi's earnest request and re-assumed the position of Governor-General of Korea. He resigned in June 1930 and is currently the Chairman of the Japan-Russia Association and the Chairman of the Japan Enlightenment Organizations Federation, a large federation of Japanese fascist organizations (United Press Agency). Former Governor-General of Korea, Navy Admiral Viscount Saitō Makoto, once served as Navy Minister and represented Japan at the Geneva Naval Conference in 1927. Two years later, he re-assumed the position of Governor-General of Korea, a position he had previously held for eight years. In the past two years, he has lived a life of leisure and has not been much involved in politics. Although Saitō is old, his appointment as Prime

Page 10

Minister will surely bring peace and order both domestically and internationally. When he participated in the Geneva Three-Power Naval Conference in 1927, he demonstrated his diplomatic skills. He also achieved remarkable political achievements when he governed Korea. He is a man of great magnanimity and strict self-discipline. At a time when the people of the country are restless and politics are corrupt, the emergence of such talent to take charge of politics is particularly appropriate. Therefore, the navy, army, and business community all expressed satisfaction after hearing the news today (Reuters).

The Process of Recommending Saitō to Form a Cabinet 121

Yamamoto is Old, Hiranuma is Biased

Saionji Decisively Suppresses the Political Tide

National News Agency, Tokyo, 22nd: Since Duke Saionji arrived in Kyoto, he has repeatedly met with senior statesmen and veterans over the past three days to seek their opinions on resolving the political crisis. The military, which strongly advocates overthrowing the party cabinet, and the civil servants, who advocate upholding the constitution and maintaining the party cabinet, have made their respective arguments. After carefully listening to the arguments of all parties, Saionji made a decisive decision, abandoning Hiranuma, the leader of the Kokuhonsha, who is at the center of the political tide, and Suzuki, the new president of the Seiyukai, and recommending Viscount Saitō Makoto, the former Governor-General of Korea and Navy Admiral, who is unrelated to both, to form a transcendent cabinet. This both reluctantly accedes to the military's request to form a national unity cabinet and can slightly appease the party's spirit, thereby easing the dispute as a temporary transition. Thus, at 1:30 PM today, he entered the palace to see the Emperor, presented his case for about an hour, and formally recommended Saitō to form a cabinet. The Emperor naturally approved, and the Imperial Household Agency first informed Viscount Saitō by telephone, and then Okamoto conveyed the order and formally summoned Saitō to Kyoto. Saitō then entered Kyoto around 6:00 PM that evening, met the Emperor, and received the imperial order to form a cabinet. However, since a transcendent cabinet is being formed this time, and it is in the midst of a dispute between two factions, the selection of cabinet members will be a difficult task and it is feared that it will not be possible to announce them in a short time.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 22nd: Prince Saionji received a visit from Navy Minister Osumi at 8:00 this morning, followed by a visit from Marshal Togo. At 10:20, Minister of the Imperial Household Makino visited for a final consultation. Thus, Prince Saionji's meetings with senior statesmen were completed. Regarding the next Prime Minister, there was initially talk of choosing one from among four people: Suzuki, the President of the Seiyukai; Baron Hiranuma Kiichirō; Count Yamamoto Gonnohyōe; and Saitō Makoto. Count Yamamoto, with his qualifications as a veteran, has a high reputation, and the senior statesmen unanimously recommended him. However, there are doubts as to whether he can handle this difficult task at the advanced age of 81. If Baron Hiranuma forms a cabinet, his policies will inevitably be biased towards one side, which is quite dangerous. Therefore, due to these various factors, Saitō Makoto is the most suitable candidate and has received the support of a majority of senior statesmen. Therefore, he recommended Saitō.

Military Circles Are Exuberant 122

United Press Agency, Tokyo, 22nd: It is reported that the military and the Adachi faction are both satisfied with the appointment of Viscount Saitō to form a cabinet. Zhongye and Otsuka, etc., from the Adachi faction, gathered at Adachi's residence to discuss countermeasures.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 22nd: Regarding the next cabinet, the main body within the Army Department insists that the next cabinet should belong to an established political party. If it can realize the reality of a national unity cabinet, it will not object to its people. The young officers argue that the occurrence of this unfortunate incident is due to the corruption of the established political parties, so they absolutely oppose anyone with party membership in the established political parties. The two factions were initially opposed to each other. Recently, the main body has strongly consoled the young officers, arguing that if things are done as the young officers advocate, the political situation will only become more chaotic, and the responsibility must be borne by the military. Currently, the general trend in the military is that unless it is a cabinet of Suzuki alone, the strong arguments from the past can be expected to soften somewhat.

Resignation of the Greek Cabinet 128

Mainly due to Financial Problems

National General Strike Begins

National News Agency, Athens, 21st – The Greek cabinet resigned today. Government agencies are at a standstill due to a general strike by all employees. Government personnel are demanding a general pay raise. The government authorities have mobilized strong military forces to guard government agencies and have set up machine guns to prevent any unforeseen events.

National News Agency, Athens, 21st – After the resignation of the Venizelos cabinet, Mr. Venizelos advocated for the formation of a coalition government, including representatives of the royalist party, believing that this was the only way to cope with the current situation. The government recently promulgated a new press law prohibiting newspapers from criticizing the authorities, which has met with strong opposition from the people. It is now believed that this is one of the reasons for the cabinet's resignation. The strike wave is worsening, with postal and telecommunications partially disrupted, and telephone service completely cut off nationwide. The army's radio stations are now providing round-the-clock service to maintain intelligence communication between the government and local officials in various provinces. Some officials in inland tax offices have also joined the strike, and there have been several clashes between strikers and the military. There are fears that the unrest will spread to all of Thessaly and Macedonia. The authorities have dispatched additional warships to the troubled areas.

Reuters, Athens, 21st – The Greek government resigned today due to financial difficulties and the suspension of foreign debt payments. It is reported that before resigning, the government sent letters to the governments of Britain, France, and Italy, expressing concerns that it would be forced to over-issue currency, leading to a sharp devaluation of the currency.

Greek and Austrian Finances on the Brink of Bankruptcy 129

Reuters, London, 22nd – The financial situation of Austria and Greece is on the verge of collapse, making everyone increasingly aware that the Lausanne reparations conference is urgently needed to prevent a major disaster from spreading. However, negotiations are now at least underway. It is now believed that Britain's policy aims to create an atmosphere advocating for gradual global improvement rather than seeking immediate and massive effects. For example, Britain is now trying to extend the Hoover moratorium plan to allow for more permanent negotiations after the U.S. elections. It is also seeking to achieve a genuine understanding between France and Germany and to seize the opportunity to transform it into a "Super Locarno" conference. However, judging from the remarks of former French Prime Minister Herriot, this goal has not yet been achieved, as Mr. Herriot stated that French foreign policy would not change due to changes in government. However, according to well-informed French reporters, France is now considering: (1) Reparations and Allied war debts can be suspended but not canceled; (2) Reduce military spending before the results of the disarmament conference; (3) Implement a major development of the Danube plan, allowing France, Poland, Italy, and Germany to share the benefits. From this, it can be seen that France also attaches great importance to the Lausanne conference.

Reuters, London, 21st – The Athens International Financial Committee has formally protested to the Greek government for failing to fulfill its foreign debt obligations. The British representative also participated in this protest. The British government has now received a reply from the Greek government stating that due to Greece's financial difficulties, the government had no choice but to temporarily not convert the funds due on May 1st for foreign debt payments into foreign currency. If it continues to repay foreign debts, the only way to make up for the budget deficit would be to issue more banknotes, which would cause the price of Greek currency to plummet due to the over-issuance of banknotes. The Greek government hopes to temporarily suspend foreign debt payments pending the outcome of the Lausanne conference and seek an agreement with the creditor nations. At that time, Greece will do its utmost to propose a satisfactory solution that will benefit the creditors. The Greek government is prepared to submit the entire issue to arbitration to determine Greece's ability to repay its debts. It is reported that the French and Italian governments have also received similar replies from Greece.

Reuters, Geneva, 22nd – The League of Nations Administrative Council met today to discuss the poverty of Eastern European countries, but without result. It only passed a resolution asking Austria and Greece to make every effort to respect all obligations while the League of Nations Financial Committee discusses their difficulties.

Amelia Earhart Flies Solo Across the Atlantic 130

Covering Two Thousand Miles in Sixteen Hours

Mrs. Putnam Completes her Ambitious Goal

Reuters, London, 21st – Mrs. Putnam, the first female aviator to fly solo across the Atlantic, landed near Londonderry in Ireland, having flown a straight line of two thousand miles in sixteen hours, a new record. When she departed from Newfoundland, she told people, "You can hear good news from me in fifteen hours." Her words proved true. Five years ago, Colonel Lindbergh made a similar feat, reaching Paris directly. Mrs. Putnam's flight ended in Ireland due to a leaking fuel tank. News of her success was warmly welcomed by people in New York, London, and Paris. Her husband, a prominent publisher in New York, told Reuters, "I knew she could do it." Mrs. Putnam, 34, whose original name was O'Herte, married last year. People call her the female Lindbergh because her flying achievements are very similar to those of Colonel Lindbergh. The only food she took on her voyage was a bottle of chicken broth. It has been fifteen times before that the Atlantic has been crossed from west to east, but Mrs. Putnam is the first to fly two thousand miles in sixteen hours. Four years ago, Mrs. Putnam flew across the Atlantic for the first time with two aviators. She then engaged in social work in the United States, but still practiced flying from time to time. Mrs. Putnam has now received many congratulatory telegrams from all over the world.

Reuters, Washington, 21st – President Hoover has telegraphed Mrs. Putnam to congratulate her on her successful solo flight across the Atlantic.

Havas, London, 21st – Female aviator Mrs. Putnam successfully crossed the Atlantic on the fifth anniversary of Colonel Lindbergh's crossing of the Atlantic, which is why the entire United States is particularly jubilant.

During the meeting, Lord Lytton asked questions and Li answered, as follows: (Question) After the establishment of "Manchukuo", has there been any reorganization of the situation in Jilin? I would like to know. (Answer) Jilin has gradually reorganized after the establishment of the new country, and all politics have progressed. (Question) I heard that the currency system in Jilin is very chaotic. What is the reason? (Answer) The currency system in Jilin is a local system, with two types of official notes and Yongda Yang, which are inconvertible paper currencies, and their credit has been greatly reduced, which is why they are chaotic. (Question) Does the chaos of the currency system cause losses to the people? (Answer) Of course the people suffer losses. In the past, two strings and five hundred cash could be exchanged for one silver dollar, but now one silver dollar can be exchanged for more than five hundred and eighty strings, which is very different from the past. (Question) I understand. The chaos of Jilin official notes is the same reason as the chaos of Fengda Yang, but are there any ways to improve and remedy it? (Answer) The new country is now planning to build a bank to recover local paper currency, and is in the process of preparation. (Question) How many types of taxes and levies are there in Jilin, and have there been any facts of increased taxes and levies after the incident? (Answer) The types of taxes and levies in Jilin are roughly land tax, sales tax, and consumption tax. There have been no increases after the incident, and the 20% military expenditure added by the warlords has been exempted. (Question) What kinds of suffering did the people suffer from the warlords in the past? (Answer) Due to the large number of troops trained and the large number of guns purchased, the currency system was chaotic, bandits multiplied, many bandits were attracted, and corruption and perversion of the law were innumerable. (Question) Have the people suffered from the Kuomintang? (Answer) Fortunately, the Kuomintang people in Jilin did not stay long, and their policies were not implemented, otherwise, of course, the people would have suffered. (Question) What is the recent bandit situation in Jilin Province? I don't know if there is a way to deal with it? (Answer) The bandits in Jilin are currently being suppressed. At this point, Lord Lytton stood up, shook hands and said goodbye. At 3:30 PM, he arrived at Jilin Station and boarded the original train to leave Jilin. (8th)

Our county suffered from a major flood last year, and the fields were submerged. This spring, disasters remain everywhere. Director Shen of the Education Department Arrives at the Department to Take Office

Education Sector Resigns, Demanding Back Pay, Rejection

Hankou Correspondence: After Shen Shiyuan, Director of the Education Department, took office on the 18th, the teachers and staff of various schools and museums still firmly opposed him. After the decision of the representative assembly, on the 19th, they all resigned from their respective schools and museums and demanded back pay. On the following day, the following formally suspended classes and work: First Middle School, Third Middle School, Ninth Middle School, Twelfth Middle School, First Women's Middle School, Women's Normal School, Rural Normal School, Provincial Normal School, First Elementary School, Third Elementary School, Fourth Elementary School, Fifth Elementary School, Seventh Elementary School, Eighth Elementary School, Fourteenth Elementary School, Fifteenth Elementary School, Experimental Public Education Center, Science Experiment Center, Municipal Vocational School, Municipal First Elementary School, Third Elementary School, Fourth Elementary School, Fifth Elementary School, Seventh Elementary School, Eighth Elementary School, Second Vocational Supplementary School, and various elementary schools, a total of 31 schools and museums. The following decided to continue suspending classes and work: Provincial Male Vocational School, Municipal First Women's Middle School, Provincial Tenth Elementary School, Municipal First Male Middle School, Municipal Sixth Elementary School, Municipal Experimental Museum, Provincial Library, and other 7 schools and museums. The following decided not to stop: Provincial High School, Second Middle School, Second Women's Middle School, Provincial Experimental School, Provincial Female Vocational School, and Sixth Elementary School, a total of 6 schools. At the same time, a declaration rejecting Shen was issued, stating, "Mr. Shen is a person who is good at inciting tides and has no knowledge. Even a three-foot-tall child knows that he is not qualified to be a role model for young people. The public is angry and unanimously rejects him. Unexpectedly, Shen ignored this and shamelessly took office. In order to improve Hubei education and fight for the personality of the education sector, how can we allow Shen to fulfill his personal wishes and occupy an important position? We can only resign entirely, demand the clearing of arrears, in order to preserve our personality and seek justice. Our will is unified, our attitude is bright, heaven and earth can testify, and the facts can prove it. As for the consequences of this resignation, such as the interruption of education and the loss of schooling for young people, Mr. Shen alone should be responsible." The principals of various schools and museums, due to the resignation of all teachers and staff, have no way to carry out their work, so they also convened a meeting and decided to resign to the provincial government. The uproar has become even more difficult to deal with. More than 10,000 middle and elementary school students cannot but declare their abandonment of school. After this incident occurred, the attitudes of various parties were quite noteworthy. Xia Douyin, chairman of the provincial government, on the one hand, respected the central government's orders and maintained Shen's arrival, and on the other hand, tried to find a peaceful solution. He scheduled to convene representatives of teachers and staff to the government on the 21st to talk, and invited provincial committee member Kong Geng and Secretary-General Yang Zaichun to negotiate on behalf of the government, in order to prevent the tide from expanding further. The Pacification Commissioner's Office believed that the teachers and staff rejected Shen and failed to always adopt the procedure of petitioning, and actually issued leaflets, causing social suspicion. During this martial law period, it should be prohibited. On the 20th, it ordered the garrison headquarters to investigate and prohibit them. As for public opinion, newspapers published as much information as possible from both sides, and some also commented on the matter. They could express support for the rejection of Shen, but they believed that it was inappropriate to use the strike as a means, causing more than 10,000 young people to lose their schooling, and called it a suicide policy to promote the education sector's reform.

Recent Situation of the Zhejiang Provincial Library 137

Since Chen Xunci was appointed director of the Zhejiang Provincial Library by the Education Department this spring, he has actively reorganized the library's internal affairs. The number of readers and the purchase of new books have greatly increased compared to before. The recent situation of the library's various groups is briefly described below: (1) Reading Group: The two sections of cataloging and lending continue to operate as usual, but there are many improvements in the arrangement compared to before. As for the cataloging work, in addition to dealing with new books, the old books in the library were mostly incompletely cataloged. Now, the library is considering the importance of things and first sorting out the general categories of books (thread-bound books), determining the category numbers, and adding borrowing bags, borrowing slips, and various book cards to facilitate checking. (2) Collection Group: Currently, it is limited to purchasing and receiving donations. There is no transfer of seals yet. Systematic purchasing will also have to wait until the sorting of the old books is completed before it can be used as a basis for making additional purchases. (3) Promotion Group: The main categories are book circulation and guidance. As for the most recent activities: (1) Book Circulation Matters: In addition to managing and improving the book circulation department and the public newspaper and reading center, it is also planned to establish a lending management office and hold book exhibitions, which are currently in progress. (2) Guidance Work: Organizing a guidance committee, conducting correspondence research, and planning to undertake academic lectures as appropriate. The personnel of this group have now set off to various counties and cities in Zhejiang Province to carry out guidance work. (3) Preparing to hold the First District Library Association, which is scheduled to be held at the main library in West Lake on the 22nd of this month. On that day, the president of Zhejiang University, Cheng Tianfang, will also be invited to give a lecture. (4) Editing Group: (1) Compiling and printing a monthly journal with content including academic essays, special reports, book and newspaper abstracts, library news, library affairs, an overview of domestic libraries, correspondence research, etc. Two issues have been published, each priced at one jiao per copy. (2) Revising the Overview, which contains information on all aspects of the library, will be published in the second half of the year. The one-page guide is in the form of a leaflet, with concise descriptions, and is distributed to tourists and visitors. It has been published. Other plans include revising the Rare Book Series and preparing the Zhejiang Journal. (3) Printing House: Reorganized from the old government book bureau, it sells bureau-published books, limited to those printed in-house. In August of the 18th year, a letterpress printing department was added. It now has a letterpress printing department, a book printing department, and a bookstore. The book printing department's storage location is in Zhongzheng Lane, storing 150,000 blocks of editions. The letterpress printing department is in Shuilusi Lane, with two large printing presses and more than 30 workers. Since this spring, business has been more developed than before.

Protecting Educational Administrative Personnel in Zhejiang Province 138

Restrictions on Accusers

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education, considering that educational administrative personnel bear the significant mission of improving and promoting local education, and that without strict legal protection, capable, proactive, and dedicated individuals are often subject to urging and reorganization, easily incurring blame, which is not as good as those who procrastinate and muddle through, who can remain in their positions for a long time, thereby inevitably discouraging their ambition and affecting their careers, which is extremely serious, has specially formulated measures to protect educational administrative personnel from accusations, and to impose restrictions. (1) Accusations against officials must have reliable guarantors, which has long been clearly stipulated. However, in reality, most of these guarantee letters are forged. For the sake of convenience, henceforth, accusations against educational administrative personnel must, in principle, have guarantors from the provincial capital. Guarantees from county towns and various townships must have formal certificates from local chambers of commerce or village committees to prevent the fraudulent use of letters. (2) If accusations against educational administrative personnel are found to be clearly false accusations, the Department of Education should forward the case to the provincial government, requesting the Higher Court to order local judicial organs to strictly punish the accusers in accordance with the law.

Local News

County Education Bureau Issues Order on Measures for Clearing and Supplementing Accumulated Education Expenses 139

The Shanghai County Education Bureau yesterday issued instructions to schools at all levels and various social education institutions, stating, "Received Shanghai County Government Instruction No. 293, which forwards Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Instruction No. 439, stating, 'Upon investigation, the method for clearing accumulated debts in various counties was previously formulated by this department in May of the nineteenth year (1930) as the 'Measures for Clearing Accumulated Educational Expenses Before the Eighteenth Year (1929) in Various Counties,' and issued to various counties for compliance. However, in handling this matter, various counties often use the current year's educational revenue solely to repay old debts first, resulting in insufficient funds to maintain the current year's operations and projects, sometimes with a shortfall of seven or eight months. Consequently, old debts are not cleared, and new debts accumulate, and educational staff are solely focused on collecting debts, neglecting their duties, which seriously affects education, which is no minor matter. Moreover, the repaid old debts often lack approved expenditure budgets or departmental orders as a basis, which is particularly inappropriate. Therefore, supplementary measures are further determined as follows: (1) When clearing old debts, each county should clearly delineate the year in which the debt was incurred and should only use the supplemented collection of uncollected educational fees from that year to repay the debt. If the amount of the old debt exceeds the amount that should have been collected but was not, other methods should be used to clear the debt, so as not to hinder the progress of each year's operations. (2) Each county should clear old debts after achieving a certain amount of the supplemented collection of educational fees as stipulated in the preceding article, and issue payments regularly for one year. If full repayment cannot be achieved, it should be amortized over several years, but the current year's revenue should not be diverted to repay the old debts, causing the educational projects being undertaken to become unsustainable. (3) The old debts referred to in the preceding two articles are limited to those listed in the handover of successive education bureau chiefs, which can be verified with the education bureau's revenue and expenditure accounts, approved budgets, or departmental orders. If, after the establishment of the budget, a tight budget or measures for contraction need to be set separately due to disasters, the previously set budget will become ineffective. (4) Within the scope of the preceding article, the county magistrate should supervise the director of the education bureau or the head of the education section to list the old debts in accordance with Article 2 of the 'Measures for Clearing Accumulated Educational Expenses Before the Eighteenth Year (1929) in Various Counties' and submit them for record. Those not within the scope of the preceding article will not be recognized. (5) These supplementary measures apply to arrears and delayed payments incurred after the nineteenth year (1930). In addition to distributing this to various departments, you are hereby instructed to comply, and to instruct the education bureau to comply accordingly. If the current year's funds are diverted to repay old debts or unfounded debts are recklessly recognized and arbitrarily issued, both the county magistrate and the education bureau director shall be held responsible.'"

Record of Striking the Bell in an Ancient Temple (3) The Reclusive Monk Does Not Remove the Weeds in the Courtyard 140

(IV)

How can I not be sad? The people who were awakened by my bell to farm and work are now, in broad daylight, either joyfully "eating lunch" or frowning with worry, "having no food to eat." Thinking of this, even my hands are trembling. How can I have the strength to strike this sorrowful bell again? However, I don't have the courage to resign from the monastery and strike the bell, because if I don't strike the bell, I won't have anything to eat. Strike it then! Heartlessly strike it! From now on, the sound of the bell I strike will no longer represent the cheers of those who have food to eat, but the sighs of those who have no food to eat.

(V)

I shouldn't have made my words too long. Since the bell must be struck, I have no choice but to study the method of striking it. The noon bell on a sunny day seems to be able to be struck accurately, but what about cloudy days? What about at night? These are indeed troubling questions for me.

When I was a child, I heard that ancient people used clepsydras to tell time. One day, seeing the water dripping from the eaves during the rain, I wanted to try to make a clepsydra using this principle. Soon, I had considerable success. I made a cylindrical vessel, filled it with water, and opened a small hole at the bottom, allowing the water to drip down drop by drop. The vessel was twenty-four inches high, representing twenty-four hours. Each inch was equally divided into two, representing forty-eight hours. It could be used for two days and two nights. The first time, I had to align the sun's shadow with the noon line before letting the water start dripping. When it dripped to about twelve inches, it would be noon the next day, and when it dripped to the last drop, it would be noon the day after. It could be used on cloudy days and at night. However, it was not easy to accurately tell time with this thing. When the water level was high, the pressure was high and it dripped quickly. When the water level was low, the pressure was low and it dripped slowly. Dry or humid weather affected its speed. At first, I completely trusted it and was often misled by it. Only if it was manufactured skillfully and used cleverly could it provide some assistance. This was only possible after repeated trials and verifications. But the most accurate clock at night was not the water in the vessel, but the stars in the sky. Usually, I relied on the movement of the constellations in the sky to strike my evening bell and my morning bell.

Redemption, etc. Therefore, I hereby instruct the said bureau director to follow this instruction, etc., and order compliance.

Disaster victims relied on it for relief, and the military relied on it for assistance. Its loyalty, courage, perseverance, and outstanding achievements fully demonstrated the spirit of service of our Boy Scouts and are highly commendable to society. In addition to the headquarters separately determining award measures to show encouragement, we hereby send a telegram of condolences. Chinese Boy Scout Headquarters, Jia Yin."

Closing of Wang Jiyuan's Miniature Painting Exhibition 142

Wang Jiyuan's miniature painting exhibition, held at the Jiyuan Xunqin Painting Studio at No. 90 Luban Road, McTyeire Road, has been open for several days and was previously reported. Xiao Renyuan's "Record of German Railway Investigation" 143

Mr. Xiao Renyuan, the former director of the Beijing-Hankou Railway Bureau, was sent by the Ministry of Railways to Europe and the United States three years ago to investigate railway operations. Mr. Xiao first went to Germany, then traveled to various large and small states in Europe, either interning at railway bureaus or conducting investigations in various places. He has now returned to Shanghai from the United States and has already written a large book, "Record of German Railway Investigation." The observations are accurate, and the content is rich. It covers all aspects of Germany's latest railway management, rolling stock, engineering, machinery, accounting, and data collection in detail, with over a hundred tables and over fifty exquisite illustrations. An appendix, "World Transportation," provides a detailed overview of transportation in various countries. It can serve as a compass for China's future railway industry. The book has already been published, priced at one dollar and fifty cents in paperback, and is managed by the Shanghai Life Weekly Society, the Youth Association Bookstore, and major bookstores such as Xinyue and Kaiming.
